<

Built for designing.

Welcome to your custom build of Tachyons.

Create fast loading, highly readable, and 100% responsive interfaces with as little css as possible.

Getting Started

Copy the link style tag and paste it it in the head of the html file(s) you want to include this custom tachyons build in 

<html lang="en">
  <title> </title>
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://tachyons.pub/0.25.0/e0dae3036b6b78ca01f0941a1d786c02/css/tachyons.min.css" />
  <body>
  </body>
</html>

Start Using

/*
  TYPE SCALE
  Docs: http://tachyons.io/docs/typography/scale/

  Base:
    f = font-size

  Modifiers:
    1 = 1st step in size scale
    2 = 2nd step in size scale
    3 = 3rd step in size scale
    4 = 4th step in size scale
    5 = 5th step in size scale
    6 = 6th step in size scale
    7 = 7th step in size scale
    8 = 8th step in size scale
    9 = 9th step in size scale

  Media Query Extensions:
    -s  = 20em
    -ns  = 40em
    -m  = 40em
    -l  = 64em
    -xl  = 80em
*/
.g-f1 { font-size: 0.75rem; }
.g-f2 { font-size: 0.875rem; }
.g-f3 { font-size: 1rem; }
.g-f4 { font-size: 1.25rem; }
.g-f5 { font-size: 1.5rem; }
.g-f6 { font-size: 2rem; }
.g-f7 { font-size: 2.25rem; }
.g-f8 { font-size: 2.5rem; }
.g-f9 { font-size: 5rem; }

/*

  TYPOGRAPHY
  http://tachyons.io/docs/typography/measure/

  Measures:
    measure = literal value 20em (base line length)
    measure-narrow = literal value 30em (narrow line length)
    measure-wide = literal value 34em (wide line length)

  Media Query Extensions:
    -s  = 20em
    -ns  = 40em
    -m  = 40em
    -l  = 64em
    -xl  = 80em

*/
